I.-Introduction_NN ._.
The_DT death-rate_NN from_IN Malaria_NNP in_IN the_DT Punjab_NNP is_VBZ always_RB a_DT large_JJ one_CD ,_, but_CC from_IN time_NN to_TO time_NN it_PRP reaches_VBZ a_DT very_RB high_JJ figure_NN ,_, as_IN in_IN the_DT year_NN 1908_CD and_CC in_IN the_DT year_NN under_IN review_NN ._.
There_EX were_VBD 697,058_CD fever_JJ deaths_NNS in_IN the_DT year_NN 1908_CD ,_, out_IN of_IN a_DT total_JJ number_NN of_IN 1,020,125_CD ._.
In_IN 1917_CD the_DT number_NN of_IN fever_JJ deaths_NNS was_VBD 510,812_CD and_CC the_DT total_JJ number_NN 733_CD ,_, 109_CD ._.
2_CD ._.
Though_IN all_PDT the_DT deaths_NNS reported_VBD as_IN from_IN fevers_NNS were_VBD not_RB necessarily_RB due_JJ to_TO malaria_NNS ,_, it_PRP is_VBZ probable_JJ that_IN these_DT figures_NNS represent_VBP more_JJR truly_RB the_DT immensity_NN of_IN the_DT mortality_NN caused_VBN directly_RB or_CC indirectly_RB by_IN this_DT infection_NN than_IN for_IN instance_NN to_TO those_DT referable_JJ to_TO plague_VB ._.
3_CD ._.
The_DT indirect_JJ effect_NN of_IN malaria_NN on_IN the_DT mortality_NN rate_NN is_VBZ probably_RB more_RBR to_TO be_VB feared_VBN than_IN the_DT direct_JJ ._.
It_PRP would_MD be_VB difficult_JJ to_TO give_VB any_DT idea_NN of_IN its_PRP$ malign_NN influence_NN on_IN the_DT causation_NN of_IN deaths_NNS in_IN infancy_NN and_CC on_IN those_DT due_JJ ostensibly_RB to_TO respiratory_NN diseases_NNS ._.
It_PRP certainly_RB has_VBZ a_DT serious_JJ effect_NN on_IN the_DT birth-rate_NN and_CC on_IN the_DT expectation_NN of_IN life_NN ,_, while_IN it_PRP is_VBZ the_DT greatest_JJS of_IN all_PDT the_DT causes_NNS for_IN disability_NN and_CC inefficiency_NN in_IN the_DT adult_NN ._.
II.-GENERAL_JJ CONSIDERATIONS_NNP ._.
4_CD ._.
The_DT total_JJ number_NN of_IN deaths_NNS from_IN fever_NN was_VBD 510,812_CD against_IN 376,003_CD in_IN 1916_CD and_CC 284,784_CD in_IN 1915_CD giving_VBG a_DT death-rate_JJ respectively_NN of_IN 26.42_CD ,_, 19.44_CD and_CC 14.72_CD ._.
5_CD ._.

6_CD ._.
There_EX were_VBD 91,505_CD more_JJR deaths_NNS in_IN 1917_CD than_IN in_IN any_DT one_CD of_IN the_DT last_JJ 17_CD years_NNS excepting_VBG in_IN the_DT great_JJ epidemic_NN of_IN 1908_CD ._.
7_CD ._.
The_DT total_JJ number_NN of_IN deaths_NNS from_IN ``_`` Fevers_NNS ``_`` was_VBD 510,812_CD ,_, while_IN from_IN all_DT causes_NNS this_DT amounted_VBD to_TO 733,109_CD ,_, the_DT corresponding_JJ death-rates_NNS being_VBG 26.42_CD and_CC 37.91_CD ,_, respectively_RB ;_: thus_RB ``_`` Fevers_NNS ''_'' were_VBD responsible_JJ for_IN more_JJR than_IN 5/7th_CD of_IN the_DT total_JJ deaths_NNS in_IN the_DT Province_NNP ._.

III.-METEOROLOGICAL_JJ FEATURES_NNP OF_IN THE_NNP PUNJAB_NNP FOR_NNP 1917_CD ._.
9_CD ._.
During_IN the_DT first_JJ two_CD months_NNS the_DT rainfall_NN was_VBD either_RB wanting_VBG altogether_RB or_CC much_RB below_IN normal_JJ ;_: the_DT month_NN of_IN March_NNP was_VBD relatively_RB drier_JJ and_CC the_DT fall_NN defective_JJ though_IN the_DT precipitation_NN exceeded_VBD that_IN of_IN the_DT months_NNS of_IN January_NNP and_CC February_NNP ._.
The_DT rainfall_NN in_IN April_NNP was_VBD ,_, though_IN late_JJ ,_, abnormally_RB high_JJ ._.
The_DT month_NN of_IN May_NNP was_VBD noticeable_JJ for_IN a_DT number_NN of_IN dust-storms_NNS and_CC thunder-storms_NNS and_CC the_DT rainfall_NN was_VBD much_RB above_IN the_DT average_NN ._.
The_DT monsoon_NN broke_VBD as_RB early_JJ as_IN the_DT 2nd_CD June_NNP and_CC spread_NN to_TO the_DT whole_NN of_IN the_DT Province_NNP ;_: and_CC there_EX were_VBD general_JJ rains_NNS on_IN the_DT 2nd_CD ,3rd_NN ,_, 7th_CD ,_, 17th_CD to_TO 20th_CD and_CC 29th_CD of_IN June_NNP and_CC the_DT total_JJ monthly_JJ rainfall_NN was_VBD 1.15_CD ''_'' above_IN the_DT average_NN ._.
The_DT precipitation_NN in_IN July_NNP was_VBD about_IN the_DT normal_JJ in_IN the_DT south-west_JJ ,_, but_CC was_VBD more_JJR marked_JJ in_IN the_DT north_NN and_CC east_NN ._.
The_DT rainfall_NN was_VBD far_RB in_IN excess_JJ generally_RB during_IN the_DT months_NNS of_IN August_NNP and_CC September_NNP ,_, the_DT total_NN for_IN the_DT whole_NN of_IN the_DT province_NN being_VBG in_IN excess_NN of_IN the_DT normal_JJ by_IN 4_CD ''_'' or_CC 75_CD per_IN cent_NN ._.
in_IN the_DT former_JJ months_NNS ,_, and_CC 8_CD 1/4_CD ''_'' or_CC 306_CD per_IN cent_NN ._.
in_IN the_DT latter_NN ._.
